### 9.1 Memoria Breve Termine (Working Memory)

**Ruolo**: Gestione dei comandi e contesto in tempo reale.

```python
class ShortTermMemory:
    """
    Memoria di lavoro per gestione real-time.
    Mantiene il contesto della conversazione attiva.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, max_items: int = 15, session_timeout: float = 1800):
        self.buffer: List[MemoryItem] = []
        self.max_items = max_items
        self.session_timeout = session_timeout  # 30 minuti
        self.session_start = datetime.now()
        self.current_context: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    
    def add(self, item: MemoryItem) -> None:
        """Aggiunge un item alla memoria di lavoro."""
        item.timestamp = datetime.now()
        self.buffer.append(item)
        
        # Mantieni solo gli ultimi N items
        if len(self.buffer) > self.max_items:
            self.buffer = self.buffer[-self.max_items:]
        
        # Aggiorna contesto corrente
        self._update_context(item)
    
    def get_recent(self, n: int = 5) -> List[MemoryItem]:
        """Ottieni gli ultimi N messaggi."""
        return self.buffer[-n:]
    
    def get_context(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Restituisce il contesto attuale della conversazione.
        
        Esempio output:
        {
            "topic": "ottimizzazione sistema",
            "entities": ["RAM", "Chrome", "processi"],
            "user_intent": "risolvere lentezza PC",
            "last_actions": ["check_memory", "list_processes"],
            "conversation_turns": 5
        }
        """
        return {
            "topic": self._extract_topic(),
            "entities": self._extract_entities(),
            "user_intent": self._infer_intent(),
            "last_actions": self._get_recent_actions(),
            "conversation_turns": len(self.buffer)
        }
    
    def search(self, query: str) -> List[MemoryItem]:
        """Cerca nella memoria breve termine."""
        results = []
        query_lower = query.lower()
        
        for item in self.buffer:
            if query_lower in item.content.lower():
                results.append(item)
        
        return results
    
    def clear_session(self) -> None:
        """Pulisce la sessione corrente."""
        self.buffer.clear()
        self.current_context.clear()
        self.session_start = datetime.now()
    
    def is_session_expired(self) -> bool:
        """Verifica se la sessione Ã¨ scaduta."""
        elapsed = (datetime.now() - self.session_start).total_seconds()
        return elapsed > self.session_timeout
```

**Contenuto Working Memory**:

| Tipo | Dati | TTL |
|------|------|-----|
| **Messaggi Utente** | Ultimi 10-15 messaggi | Sessione |
| **Risposte Sistema** | Ultime risposte JARVIS/GIDEON | Sessione |
| **Azioni Recenti** | Comandi eseguiti | Sessione |
| **EntitÃ  Estratte** | Nomi, app, path menzionati | Sessione |
| **Intent Corrente** | Obiettivo utente attivo | Fino a completamento |

---

### 9.2 Memoria Lungo Termine (Persistent Knowledge)

**Ruolo**: Apprendimento dai risultati e aggiornamento strategie.

```python
class LongTermMemory:
    """
    Memoria persistente per conoscenza acquisita.
    Apprende dai risultati e ottimizza strategie nel tempo.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, storage_path: Path):
        self.storage_path = storage_path
        self.knowledge_base: Dict[str, Knowledge] = {}
        self.strategies: Dict[str, Strategy] = {}
        self.user_preferences: UserPreferences = UserPreferences()
        self._load()
    
    def store_learning(
        self,
        category: str,
        key: str,
        value: Any,
        confidence: float = 0.5,
        source: str = "observation"
    ) -> None:
        """
        Memorizza un apprendimento.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> memory.store_learning(
        ...     category="user_preferences",
        ...     key="preferred_browser",
        ...     value="Chrome",
        ...     confidence=0.9,
        ...     source="explicit_statement"
        ... )
        """
        knowledge = Knowledge(
            category=category,
            key=key,
            value=value,
            confidence=confidence,
            source=source,
            learned_at=datetime.now(),
            access_count=0,
            last_accessed=None
        )
        
        # Se esiste giÃ , aggiorna con decay
        existing = self.knowledge_base.get(f"{category}:{key}")
        if existing:
            knowledge = self._merge_knowledge(existing, knowledge)
        
        self.knowledge_base[f"{category}:{key}"] = knowledge
        self._persist()
    
    def update_strategy(
        self,
        action_type: str,
        outcome: ActionOutcome,
        context: Dict[str, Any]
    ) -> None:
        """
        Aggiorna strategia basata su outcome.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> memory.update_strategy(
        ...     action_type="optimize_memory",
        ...     outcome=ActionOutcome(success=True, improvement=0.3),
        ...     context={"ram_usage": 0.85, "method": "close_chrome_tabs"}
        ... )
        """
        strategy_key = action_type
        
        if strategy_key not in self.strategies:
            self.strategies[strategy_key] = Strategy(
                action_type=action_type,
                success_patterns=[],
                failure_patterns=[],
                best_contexts=[]
            )
        
        strategy = self.strategies[strategy_key]
        
        if outcome.success:
            strategy.success_patterns.append({
                "context": context,
                "improvement": outcome.improvement,
                "timestamp": datetime.now()
            })
            # Identifica pattern di successo
            self._analyze_success_pattern(strategy, context)
        else:
            strategy.failure_patterns.append({
                "context": context,
                "error": outcome.error,
                "timestamp": datetime.now()
            })
        
        self._persist()
    
    def get_best_strategy(
        self,
        action_type: str,
        current_context: Dict[str, Any]
    ) -> Optional[StrategyRecommendation]:
        """
        Restituisce la migliore strategia per il contesto.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> rec = memory.get_best_strategy("optimize_memory", {"ram_usage": 0.9})
        StrategyRecommendation(
            method="close_chrome_tabs",
            confidence=0.85,
            expected_improvement=0.25,
            reason="Successo 8/10 volte in contesti simili"
        )
        """
        strategy = self.strategies.get(action_type)
        if not strategy:
            return None
        
        # Trova pattern piÃ¹ simile al contesto attuale
        best_match = self._find_similar_context(
            strategy.success_patterns,
            current_context
        )
        
        if best_match:
            return StrategyRecommendation(
                method=best_match.get("method"),
                confidence=self._calculate_confidence(strategy, best_match),
                expected_improvement=best_match.get("improvement", 0),
                reason=self._generate_reason(strategy, best_match)
            )
        
        return None
    
    def recall(
        self,
        query: str,
        category: Optional[str] = None,
        min_confidence: float = 0.3
    ) -> List[Knowledge]:
        """Recupera conoscenza dalla memoria."""
        results = []
        
        for key, knowledge in self.knowledge_base.items():
            if category and not key.startswith(f"{category}:"):
                continue
            
            if knowledge.confidence < min_confidence:
                continue
            
            if self._matches_query(knowledge, query):
                knowledge.access_count += 1
                knowledge.last_accessed = datetime.now()
                results.append(knowledge)
        
        # Ordina per rilevanza e confidence
        return sorted(results, key=lambda k: k.confidence, reverse=True)
```

**Struttura Knowledge Base**:

```json
{
  "user_preferences:browser": {
    "value": "Chrome",
    "confidence": 0.95,
    "source": "explicit",
    "learned_at": "2026-01-15",
    "access_count": 47
  },
  "user_preferences:coding_language": {
    "value": "Python",
    "confidence": 0.88,
    "source": "observation",
    "learned_at": "2026-01-10"
  },
  "system:optimal_ram_threshold": {
    "value": 0.75,
    "confidence": 0.72,
    "source": "learning",
    "learned_at": "2026-01-20"
  },
  "strategies:memory_optimization": {
    "best_method": "close_browser_tabs",
    "success_rate": 0.82,
    "avg_improvement": 0.23
  }
}
```

### 9.3 Memoria Episodica

**Ruolo**: Traccia eventi, scenari e contesti storici.

```python
class EpisodicMemory:
    """
    Memoria di episodi: eventi specifici nel tempo.
    Permette di "ricordare" quando e come sono successe le cose.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, storage_path: Path, max_episodes: int = 1000):
        self.storage_path = storage_path
        self.episodes: List[Episode] = []
        self.max_episodes = max_episodes
        self.index = EpisodeIndex()
        self._load()
    
    def record_episode(
        self,
        event_type: str,
        description: str,
        context: Dict[str, Any],
        participants: List[str] = None,
        outcome: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> Episode:
        """
        Registra un episodio.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> episode = memory.record_episode(
        ...     event_type="problem_solved",
        ...     description="PC lento risolto chiudendo Chrome",
        ...     context={
        ...         "initial_ram": 0.92,
        ...         "final_ram": 0.65,
        ...         "method": "close_chrome_tabs",
        ...         "tabs_closed": 47
        ...     },
        ...     participants=["user", "jarvis", "gideon"],
        ...     outcome="success"
        ... )
        """
        episode = Episode(
            id=self._generate_id(),
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            event_type=event_type,
            description=description,
            context=context,
            participants=participants or [],
            outcome=outcome,
            embeddings=self._generate_embeddings(description, context)
        )
        
        self.episodes.append(episode)
        self.index.add(episode)
        
        # Cleanup vecchi episodi
        if len(self.episodes) > self.max_episodes:
            self._prune_old_episodes()
        
        self._persist()
        return episode
    
    def recall_similar(
        self,
        situation: str,
        context: Dict[str, Any] = None,
        limit: int = 5
    ) -> List[Episode]:
        """
        Trova episodi simili alla situazione attuale.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> episodes = memory.recall_similar(
        ...     situation="PC Ã¨ lento",
        ...     context={"ram_usage": 0.88}
        ... )
        [Episode(description="PC lento risolto chiudendo Chrome", outcome="success"),
         Episode(description="Lentezza risolta con restart", outcome="success")]
        """
        # Genera embedding per la situazione
        query_embedding = self._generate_embeddings(situation, context or {})
        
        # Cerca per similaritÃ 
        return self.index.search_similar(query_embedding, limit=limit)
    
    def recall_by_timeframe(
        self,
        start: datetime,
        end: datetime,
        event_type: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> List[Episode]:
        """Recupera episodi in un intervallo temporale."""
        results = []
        
        for episode in self.episodes:
            if start <= episode.timestamp <= end:
                if event_type is None or episode.event_type == event_type:
                    results.append(episode)
        
        return sorted(results, key=lambda e: e.timestamp)
    
    def get_outcome_statistics(
        self,
        event_type: str,
        timeframe_days: int = 30
    ) -> OutcomeStats:
        """
        Statistiche outcomes per tipo di evento.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> stats = memory.get_outcome_statistics("memory_optimization", 30)
        OutcomeStats(
            total=25,
            success=21,
            failure=4,
            success_rate=0.84,
            avg_improvement=0.22
        )
        """
        cutoff = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=timeframe_days)
        relevant = [
            e for e in self.episodes
            if e.event_type == event_type and e.timestamp > cutoff
        ]
        
        successes = sum(1 for e in relevant if e.outcome == "success")
        
        return OutcomeStats(
            total=len(relevant),
            success=successes,
            failure=len(relevant) - successes,
            success_rate=successes / len(relevant) if relevant else 0,
            avg_improvement=self._calc_avg_improvement(relevant)
        )
```

**Tipi di Episodi Tracciati**:

| Evento | Dati Registrati | Uso |
|--------|-----------------|-----|
| `command_executed` | Comando, risultato, durata | Ottimizzazione risposte |
| `problem_solved` | Problema, soluzione, contesto | Pattern matching futuro |
| `error_occurred` | Errore, causa, fix | Prevenzione errori |
| `user_preference_learned` | Preferenza, contesto | Personalizzazione |
| `automation_run` | Routine, steps, outcome | Miglioramento automazioni |
| `scenario_simulated` | Scenari GIDEON, accuratezza | Calibrazione predizioni |

---

### 9.4 Memoria Decisionale

**Ruolo**: Apprende dai risultati delle azioni passate.

```python
class DecisionMemory:
    """
    Memoria delle decisioni: traccia decisioni e loro outcome.
    Permette di migliorare le decisioni future.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, storage_path: Path):
        self.storage_path = storage_path
        self.decisions: Dict[str, DecisionRecord] = {}
        self.outcome_tracker = OutcomeTracker()
        self._load()
    
    def record_decision(
        self,
        decision_id: str,
        intent: str,
        options_considered: List[Dict],
        chosen_option: Dict,
        reasoning: str,
        confidence: float,
        context: Dict[str, Any]
    ) -> DecisionRecord:
        """
        Registra una decisione presa.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> record = memory.record_decision(
        ...     decision_id="dec-20260128-001",
        ...     intent="optimize_performance",
        ...     options_considered=[
        ...         {"action": "close_apps", "score": 0.7},
        ...         {"action": "increase_ram", "score": 0.3},
        ...         {"action": "restart", "score": 0.5}
        ...     ],
        ...     chosen_option={"action": "close_apps", "score": 0.7},
        ...     reasoning="Minimo impatto, alta probabilitÃ  successo",
        ...     confidence=0.75,
        ...     context={"ram_usage": 0.88, "time": "working_hours"}
        ... )
        """
        record = DecisionRecord(
            id=decision_id,
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            intent=intent,
            options_considered=options_considered,
            chosen_option=chosen_option,
            reasoning=reasoning,
            confidence=confidence,
            context=context,
            outcome=None,  # Da aggiornare dopo
            feedback=None
        )
        
        self.decisions[decision_id] = record
        self._persist()
        return record
    
    def record_outcome(
        self,
        decision_id: str,
        success: bool,
        actual_result: Any,
        user_feedback: Optional[str] = None,
        metrics: Dict[str, float] = None
    ) -> None:
        """
        Registra l'outcome di una decisione.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> memory.record_outcome(
        ...     decision_id="dec-20260128-001",
        ...     success=True,
        ...     actual_result={"ram_freed": 0.2, "apps_closed": 5},
        ...     user_feedback="Perfetto, ora va meglio",
        ...     metrics={"improvement": 0.23, "duration": 5.2}
        ... )
        """
        if decision_id not in self.decisions:
            raise KeyError(f"Decision {decision_id} not found")
        
        record = self.decisions[decision_id]
        record.outcome = DecisionOutcome(
            success=success,
            actual_result=actual_result,
            metrics=metrics or {},
            recorded_at=datetime.now()
        )
        record.feedback = user_feedback
        
        # Aggiorna tracker per apprendimento
        self.outcome_tracker.track(record)
        
        self._persist()
    
    def get_similar_decisions(
        self,
        intent: str,
        context: Dict[str, Any],
        limit: int = 10
    ) -> List[DecisionRecord]:
        """
        Trova decisioni simili passate.
        Utile per informare nuove decisioni.
        """
        similar = []
        
        for record in self.decisions.values():
            if record.intent != intent:
                continue
            
            similarity = self._calculate_context_similarity(
                record.context,
                context
            )
            
            if similarity > 0.5:  # Threshold
                similar.append((similarity, record))
        
        # Ordina per similaritÃ  e restituisci i migliori
        similar.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
        return [r for _, r in similar[:limit]]
    
    def get_decision_insights(self, intent: str) -> DecisionInsights:
        """
        Analizza decisioni passate per un intent.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> insights = memory.get_decision_insights("optimize_performance")
        DecisionInsights(
            total_decisions=45,
            success_rate=0.82,
            best_option="close_apps",
            best_option_success_rate=0.91,
            common_failure_contexts=["low_disk_space"],
            recommended_confidence_threshold=0.7
        )
        """
        relevant = [
            d for d in self.decisions.values()
            if d.intent == intent and d.outcome is not None
        ]
        
        if not relevant:
            return None
        
        # Analizza successi per opzione
        option_stats = defaultdict(lambda: {"success": 0, "total": 0})
        for d in relevant:
            option = d.chosen_option.get("action", "unknown")
            option_stats[option]["total"] += 1
            if d.outcome.success:
                option_stats[option]["success"] += 1
        
        # Trova migliore opzione
        best_option = max(
            option_stats.keys(),
            key=lambda o: option_stats[o]["success"] / option_stats[o]["total"]
        )
        
        return DecisionInsights(
            total_decisions=len(relevant),
            success_rate=sum(1 for d in relevant if d.outcome.success) / len(relevant),
            best_option=best_option,
            best_option_success_rate=option_stats[best_option]["success"] / option_stats[best_option]["total"],
            common_failure_contexts=self._analyze_failure_contexts(relevant),
            recommended_confidence_threshold=self._calc_optimal_threshold(relevant)
        )
```

---

### 9.5 Apprendimento Continuo

**Ruolo**: Adattamento automatico basato su feedback e risultati.

```python
class ContinuousLearning:
    """
    Sistema di apprendimento continuo.
    Adatta il comportamento basandosi su feedback e outcome.
    """
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        short_term: ShortTermMemory,
        long_term: LongTermMemory,
        episodic: EpisodicMemory,
        decision: DecisionMemory
    ):
        self.short_term = short_term
        self.long_term = long_term
        self.episodic = episodic
        self.decision = decision
        
        self.learning_rate = 0.1
        self.adaptation_threshold = 0.7
        self.model_weights: Dict[str, float] = {}
    
    async def learn_from_interaction(
        self,
        interaction: Interaction
    ) -> LearningResult:
        """
        Apprende da un'interazione completata.
        
        Processo:
        1. Analizza outcome
        2. Aggiorna confidence dei modelli
        3. Identifica pattern
        4. Adatta strategie
        """
        # 1. Registra in memoria episodica
        self.episodic.record_episode(
            event_type="interaction",
            description=interaction.summary,
            context=interaction.context,
            outcome="success" if interaction.success else "failure"
        )
        
        # 2. Aggiorna memoria decisionale
        if interaction.decision_id:
            self.decision.record_outcome(
                decision_id=interaction.decision_id,
                success=interaction.success,
                actual_result=interaction.result,
                user_feedback=interaction.feedback
            )
        
        # 3. Estrai apprendimenti
        learnings = self._extract_learnings(interaction)
        
        # 4. Aggiorna memoria lungo termine
        for learning in learnings:
            self.long_term.store_learning(
                category=learning.category,
                key=learning.key,
                value=learning.value,
                confidence=learning.confidence,
                source="continuous_learning"
            )
        
        # 5. Adatta modelli se necessario
        adaptation = await self._check_adaptation_needed()
        
        return LearningResult(
            learnings=learnings,
            adaptation_triggered=adaptation,
            new_patterns=self._identify_new_patterns()
        )
    
    async def adapt_strategy(
        self,
        strategy_type: str,
        performance_data: PerformanceData
    ) -> AdaptationResult:
        """
        Adatta una strategia basandosi sulle performance.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> result = await learning.adapt_strategy(
        ...     "intent_classification",
        ...     PerformanceData(accuracy=0.72, recent_errors=["wrong_intent"])
        ... )
        AdaptationResult(
            changed=True,
            old_params={"threshold": 0.5},
            new_params={"threshold": 0.6},
            reason="Accuracy sotto target, aumento threshold"
        )
        """
        # Recupera dati storici
        historical = self._get_historical_performance(strategy_type)
        
        # Calcola trend
        trend = self._calculate_trend(historical + [performance_data])
        
        # Decidi se adattare
        if performance_data.accuracy < self.adaptation_threshold:
            # Performance sotto soglia: adatta
            new_params = self._optimize_parameters(
                strategy_type,
                historical,
                performance_data
            )
            
            return AdaptationResult(
                changed=True,
                old_params=self.model_weights.get(strategy_type, {}),
                new_params=new_params,
                reason=f"Performance {performance_data.accuracy:.2f} sotto threshold {self.adaptation_threshold}"
            )
        
        if trend == "declining":
            # Trend negativo: adatta preventivamente
            new_params = self._optimize_parameters(
                strategy_type,
                historical,
                performance_data
            )
            
            return AdaptationResult(
                changed=True,
                old_params=self.model_weights.get(strategy_type, {}),
                new_params=new_params,
                reason="Trend in calo, adattamento preventivo"
            )
        
        return AdaptationResult(changed=False, reason="Performance nella norma")
    
    def consolidate_memories(self) -> ConsolidationReport:
        """
        Consolida memorie (processo notturno/periodico).
        
        - Trasferisce pattern dalla memoria breve a lungo termine
        - Prune episodi poco rilevanti
        - Ottimizza indici
        - Aggiorna statistiche
        """
        report = ConsolidationReport()
        
        # 1. Trasferisci pattern importanti a lungo termine
        patterns = self._identify_important_patterns(self.short_term)
        for pattern in patterns:
            self.long_term.store_learning(
                category="pattern",
                key=pattern.name,
                value=pattern.definition,
                confidence=pattern.confidence
            )
            report.patterns_consolidated += 1
        
        # 2. Prune episodi vecchi/irrilevanti
        pruned = self.episodic._prune_old_episodes()
        report.episodes_pruned = pruned
        
        # 3. Aggiorna statistiche decision memory
        self.decision.outcome_tracker.recalculate_stats()
        report.stats_updated = True
        
        # 4. Ottimizza indici
        self.episodic.index.optimize()
        self.long_term._optimize_index()
        report.indexes_optimized = True
        
        return report
```

---

### 9.7 Metriche di Apprendimento

```python
class LearningMetrics:
    """Metriche per monitorare qualitÃ  apprendimento."""
    
    def calculate_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "knowledge_growth": {
                "total_items": len(self.long_term.knowledge_base),
                "new_this_week": self._count_recent_knowledge(days=7),
                "avg_confidence": self._avg_confidence()
            },
            "decision_quality": {
                "success_rate_30d": self._decision_success_rate(30),
                "improvement_trend": self._success_rate_trend(),
                "avg_confidence_delta": self._confidence_calibration()
            },
            "memory_health": {
                "episodic_count": len(self.episodic.episodes),
                "short_term_utilization": len(self.short_term.buffer) / self.short_term.max_items,
                "index_efficiency": self.episodic.index.get_efficiency()
            },
            "adaptation_stats": {
                "adaptations_this_month": self._count_adaptations(30),
                "avg_improvement_post_adapt": self._post_adaptation_improvement()
            }
        }

# Output esempio:
"""
{
  "knowledge_growth": {
    "total_items": 1247,
    "new_this_week": 43,
    "avg_confidence": 0.76
  },
  "decision_quality": {
    "success_rate_30d": 0.84,
    "improvement_trend": "+0.03",
    "avg_confidence_delta": 0.05
  },
  "memory_health": {
    "episodic_count": 892,
    "short_term_utilization": 0.73,
    "index_efficiency": 0.91
  },
  "adaptation_stats": {
    "adaptations_this_month": 7,
    "avg_improvement_post_adapt": 0.12
  }
}
"""
```

## 8. API e Integrazioni

### 8.1 API REST

**Base URL**: `http://127.0.0.1:8001/api`

#### Endpoint Chat
```http
POST /api/chat/send
Content-Type: application/json

{
  "message": "Analizza stato server",
  "mode": "COPILOT",  # opzionale
  "context": {}       # opzionale
}

Response 200:
{
  "response": "Server operativo. CPU 23%, RAM 45%...",
  "cognitive_trace": {
    "gideon_used": true,
    "analysis_time": 1.2,
    "decision": "info_request",
    "actions": []
  },
  "suggestions": ["Vuoi dettagli su processi attivi?"]
}
```

#### Endpoint Gideon (Analisi Pura)
```http
POST /api/gideon/analyze
{
  "task": "predict_system_load",
  "params": {
    "timeframe": "next_24h",
    "current_metrics": {...}
  }
}

Response:
{
  "predictions": [
    {"time": "14:00", "cpu": 65, "probability": 0.82},
    {"time": "18:00", "cpu": 89, "probability": 0.91}
  ],
  "recommendations": [
    "Schedula backup alle 03:00 (load previsto 12%)"
  ]
}
```

#### Endpoint Jarvis (Esecuzione)
```http
POST /api/jarvis/execute
{
  "action": "open_app",
  "params": {
    "app_name": "Chrome",
    "url": "github.com"
  },
  "confirm": false  # se true, ritorna plan senza eseguire
}

Response:
{
  "status": "executed",
  "result": "Chrome aperto su github.com",
  "execution_time": 0.8
}
```

#### Endpoint Sistema
```http
GET /api/system/status
Response:
{
  "mode": "COPILOT",
  "gideon_active": true,
  "jarvis_active": true,
  "uptime": 86400,
  "requests_today": 247
}

POST /api/system/mode
{
  "mode": "PILOT",
  "duration": 3600
}
```

### 8.2 WebSocket

**URL**: `ws://127.0.0.1:8001/ws`

```javascript
const ws = new WebSocket('ws://127.0.0.1:8001/ws');

// Invio messaggio
ws.send(JSON.stringify({
  type: 'text_message',
  payload: {
    text: 'Monitora CPU ogni 10 secondi'
  }
}));

// Ricezione eventi
ws.onmessage = (event) => {
  const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
  
  if (data.type === 'metric_update') {
    console.log('CPU:', data.payload.cpu);
  }
  
  if (data.type === 'action_executed') {
    console.log('Azione:', data.payload.action);
  }
};
```

### 8.3 Plugin System

**Struttura Plugin**:
```python
# plugins/my_plugin.py
from core.plugin_manager import Plugin

class MyPlugin(Plugin):
    name = "CustomAnalyzer"
    version = "1.0.0"
    
    def on_analyze(self, data):
        # Hook in GIDEON analysis
        return {
            "custom_metric": self.calculate(data)
        }
    
    def on_execute(self, action):
        # Hook pre-execution JARVIS
        if action.type == "sensitive":
            return {"allow": False, "reason": "Policy violation"}
        return {"allow": True}
    
    def calculate(self, data):
        # Custom logic
        return data['value'] * 1.5
```

**Caricamento**:
```python
from core.plugin_manager import PluginManager

pm = PluginManager()
pm.load_plugin('plugins/my_plugin.py')
pm.enable('CustomAnalyzer')
```

## 9. Sicurezza

### 9.1 Livelli di Accesso

```python
class SecurityLevel:
    PUBLIC = 0       # Solo query informative
    COPILOT = 1      # Esecuzione con conferma
    PILOT = 2        # Esecuzione autonoma
    ADMIN = 3        # Configurazione sistema
```

**Azioni per Livello**:
```python
PERMISSIONS = {
    "open_app": SecurityLevel.PUBLIC,
    "search_web": SecurityLevel.PUBLIC,
    "calculate": SecurityLevel.PUBLIC,
    
    "file_read": SecurityLevel.COPILOT,
    "file_write": SecurityLevel.COPILOT,
    "install_software": SecurityLevel.COPILOT,
    
    "system_restart": SecurityLevel.PILOT,
    "registry_edit": SecurityLevel.PILOT,
    "service_control": SecurityLevel.PILOT,
    
    "delete_system_file": SecurityLevel.ADMIN,
    "change_permissions": SecurityLevel.ADMIN,
    "network_config": SecurityLevel.ADMIN
}
```

### 9.2 Audit Logging

**Formato Log**:
```json
{
  "timestamp": "2026-01-24T15:30:45Z",
  "user": "simone@localhost",
  "mode": "COPILOT",
  "action": {
    "type": "file_delete",
    "target": "C:\\temp\\old_backup.zip",
    "size_mb": 450
  },
  "decision": {
    "gideon_analysis": {
      "risk": "LOW",
      "reasoning": "File in temp, >30 giorni"
    },
    "jarvis_decision": "EXECUTE",
    "user_confirmed": true
  },
  "result": {
    "status": "success",
    "freed_space_mb": 450,
    "duration_ms": 234
  },
  "rollback_available": false
}
```

**Kill Switch**:
```python
# Voce
"EMERGENZA STOP"
"FERMA TUTTO"

# API
POST /api/emergency/stop
{
  "reason": "Comportamento anomalo rilevato"
}

# Tastiera
CTRL + ALT + K (configurabile)
```

### 11.1 Caratteristiche Avatar

```python
class GideonAvatar3D:
    """
    Avatar 3D fedele a Gideon di The Flash.
    Sincronizzazione labiale, movimenti realistici, feedback visivo.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = "gideon_flash_replica.glb"
        self.current_state = AvatarState.IDLE
        self.glow_color = GlowColor.BLUE  # Default: idle
        
        # Componenti facciali
        self.eyes = EyeController()
        self.mouth = LipSyncController()
        self.head = HeadMovementController()
        self.expressions = ExpressionEngine()
        
        # HUD
        self.hud = HUDOverlay()
    
    def set_operational_state(self, state: OperationalState) -> None:
        """
        Imposta stato operativo con glow corrispondente.
        
        Stati e colori:
        - PILOT (attivo, esecuzione): ðŸŸ¢ VERDE
        - ANALYZING (analisi, calcolo): ðŸŸ¡ GIALLO  
        - IDLE (standby, ascolto): ðŸ”µ BLU
        - ERROR: ðŸ”´ ROSSO
        - THINKING (deep reasoning): ðŸŸ£ VIOLA pulsante
        """
        state_colors = {
            OperationalState.PILOT: GlowColor.GREEN,
            OperationalState.ANALYZING: GlowColor.YELLOW,
            OperationalState.IDLE: GlowColor.BLUE,
            OperationalState.ERROR: GlowColor.RED,
            OperationalState.THINKING: GlowColor.PURPLE
        }
        
        self.glow_color = state_colors.get(state, GlowColor.BLUE)
        self._apply_glow_effect()
        self._update_expression(state)
    
    async def speak(self, text: str, emotion: str = "neutral") -> None:
        """
        Parla con labiale sincronizzato.
        """
        # Genera audio
        audio = await self.tts.synthesize(text)
        
        # Estrai fonemi per lip sync
        phonemes = self.lip_sync.extract_phonemes(text, audio)
        
        # Anima in parallelo
        await asyncio.gather(
            self._animate_lips(phonemes),
            self._animate_head_natural(),
            self._animate_eyes_tracking(),
            self._play_audio(audio)
        )
    
    def show_calculation(self, progress: float, label: str) -> None:
        """Mostra animazione di calcolo."""
        self.hud.show_progress_bar(progress, label)
        self.set_operational_state(OperationalState.ANALYZING)
        self._play_calculation_animation()
```

### 11.2 Lip Sync e Movimenti

```python
class LipSyncController:
    """Sincronizzazione labiale realistica."""
    
    PHONEME_VISEMES = {
        # Vocali
        'A': 'viseme_aa',
        'E': 'viseme_E', 
        'I': 'viseme_I',
        'O': 'viseme_O',
        'U': 'viseme_U',
        # Consonanti
        'P': 'viseme_PP',  # Labbra chiuse
        'B': 'viseme_PP',
        'M': 'viseme_PP',
        'F': 'viseme_FF',  # Labbro inferiore
        'V': 'viseme_FF',
        'TH': 'viseme_TH',
        'S': 'viseme_SS',
        'SH': 'viseme_SS',
        'K': 'viseme_kk',
        'CH': 'viseme_CH',
        'R': 'viseme_RR',
        'L': 'viseme_nn',
        'silence': 'viseme_sil'
    }
    
    async def animate(self, phonemes: List[Phoneme]) -> None:
        """Anima labbra seguendo fonemi con timing."""
        for phoneme in phonemes:
            viseme = self.PHONEME_VISEMES.get(phoneme.symbol, 'viseme_sil')
            await self._blend_to_viseme(
                viseme,
                duration=phoneme.duration,
                intensity=phoneme.intensity
            )

class HeadMovementController:
    """Movimenti naturali della testa."""
    
    async def natural_movement(self, speaking: bool = False) -> None:
        """
        Genera movimenti naturali:
        - Micro-movimenti idle
        - Nodding durante ascolto
        - Tilt durante pensiero
        - Tracking dell'utente
        """
        if speaking:
            # Leggeri movimenti durante il parlato
            await self._subtle_nod()
            await self._slight_tilt()
        else:
            # Idle breathing movement
            await self._idle_sway()

class EyeController:
    """Controllo occhi realistico."""
    
    async def animate(self) -> None:
        """
        Animazioni occhi:
        - Blink naturale (ogni 3-5 secondi)
        - Saccadi (movimenti rapidi)
        - Tracking utente/punti focali
        - Pupille reattive a stato
        """
        await asyncio.gather(
            self._blink_cycle(),
            self._saccade_movement(),
            self._pupil_dilation()
        )
```

### 11.3 Espressioni Facciali

```python
class ExpressionEngine:
    """Gestione espressioni facciali coerenti con stato."""
    
    EXPRESSIONS = {
        OperationalState.IDLE: {
            "eyebrows": 0.0,      # Neutro
            "smile": 0.1,         # Leggero sorriso
            "eyes_wide": 0.0
        },
        OperationalState.ANALYZING: {
            "eyebrows": 0.3,      # Leggermente sollevate
            "smile": 0.0,
            "eyes_wide": 0.2,     # Concentrazione
            "blink_rate": 0.5     # Meno blink durante analisi
        },
        OperationalState.PILOT: {
            "eyebrows": 0.1,
            "smile": 0.2,         # Leggero sorriso sicuro
            "eyes_wide": 0.1,
            "intensity": 0.8      # Espressione piÃ¹ marcata
        },
        OperationalState.THINKING: {
            "eyebrows": 0.4,      # Pensieroso
            "smile": 0.0,
            "eyes_up": 0.3,       # Guarda in alto (pensiero)
            "head_tilt": 0.15
        },
        OperationalState.ERROR: {
            "eyebrows": -0.2,     # Preoccupazione
            "smile": -0.1,
            "eyes_wide": 0.3
        }
    }
    
    def apply_expression(self, state: OperationalState) -> None:
        """Applica espressione corrispondente allo stato."""
        expression = self.EXPRESSIONS.get(state, self.EXPRESSIONS[OperationalState.IDLE])
        self._blend_expression(expression, duration=0.3)
```

### 11.4 HUD e Feedback Visivo

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚                              HUD OVERLAY                                    â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
```

```python
class HUDOverlay:
    """Head-Up Display per feedback visivo."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.elements = {
            "status": StatusIndicator(),
            "progress": ProgressBar(),
            "scenarios": ScenarioDisplay(),
            "confidence": ConfidenceMeter(),
            "activity_log": ActivityLog()
        }
    
    def show_scenario_analysis(self, scenarios: List[Scenario]) -> None:
        """Mostra analisi scenari in tempo reale."""
        self.elements["scenarios"].update(scenarios)
        
        # Evidenzia best scenario
        best = max(scenarios, key=lambda s: s.probability)
        self.elements["scenarios"].highlight(best)
        
        # Aggiorna confidence
        self.elements["confidence"].set_value(best.probability)
    
    def show_calculation_animation(self) -> None:
        """Animazione durante calcolo."""
        self._show_particle_effect("calculation")
        self._show_data_streams()
        self._pulse_glow()
```

### 12.1 Sistema Vocale

```python
class VoiceInteractionSystem:
    """
    Sistema di interazione vocale naturale.
    Voce sintetica con pause, intonazioni e risposta unica finale.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.tts = TextToSpeech(
            voice="gideon_natural",
            rate=1.0,
            pitch=1.0
        )
        self.stt = SpeechToText(
            language="it-IT",
            continuous=True
        )
        self.wake_words = ["hey gideon", "gideon", "jarvis", "hey jarvis"]
        self.is_listening = False
    
    async def synthesize_response(
        self,
        text: str,
        emotion: str = "neutral"
    ) -> AudioBuffer:
        """
        Genera risposta vocale naturale.
        
        Caratteristiche:
        - Pause naturali tra frasi
        - Intonazione coerente
        - Enfasi su parole chiave
        - VelocitÃ  adattiva al contenuto
        """
        # Pre-processa testo per naturalezza
        processed = self._add_natural_pauses(text)
        processed = self._add_emphasis_markers(processed)
        
        # Imposta parametri emotivi
        params = self._get_emotion_params(emotion)
        
        # Sintetizza
        audio = await self.tts.synthesize(
            processed,
            rate=params["rate"],
            pitch=params["pitch"],
            emphasis=params["emphasis"]
        )
        
        return audio
    
    def _add_natural_pauses(self, text: str) -> str:
        """Aggiunge pause naturali."""
        # Pausa dopo punto
        text = text.replace(". ", ". <pause:300ms> ")
        # Pausa breve dopo virgola
        text = text.replace(", ", ", <pause:150ms> ")
        # Pausa per enfasi
        text = re.sub(r'\b(importante|attenzione|nota)\b', 
                      r'<pause:100ms>\1<emphasis>', text, flags=re.I)
        return text
    
    def _get_emotion_params(self, emotion: str) -> Dict:
        """Parametri vocali per emozione."""
        return {
            "neutral": {"rate": 1.0, "pitch": 1.0, "emphasis": 1.0},
            "confident": {"rate": 0.95, "pitch": 1.05, "emphasis": 1.2},
            "concerned": {"rate": 0.9, "pitch": 0.95, "emphasis": 0.9},
            "excited": {"rate": 1.1, "pitch": 1.1, "emphasis": 1.3},
            "calm": {"rate": 0.85, "pitch": 0.98, "emphasis": 0.8}
        }.get(emotion, {"rate": 1.0, "pitch": 1.0, "emphasis": 1.0})

class ResponseComposer:
    """
    Compone risposta unica finale dopo ragionamento completo.
    """
    
    async def compose_final_response(
        self,
        reasoning_result: ReasoningResult,
        gideon_analysis: GideonAnalysis,
        jarvis_decision: JarvisDecision
    ) -> str:
        """
        Genera risposta unica finale.
        NON risponde durante il ragionamento.
        
        Struttura risposta:
        1. Sintesi della richiesta compresa
        2. Risultato/Decisione principale
        3. Dettagli rilevanti (se necessari)
        4. Prossimi passi (se applicabili)
        """
        response_parts = []
        
        # Solo se c'Ã¨ qualcosa da comunicare
        if jarvis_decision.outcome == DecisionOutcome.EXECUTE:
            response_parts.append(
                self._format_execution_response(jarvis_decision)
            )
        elif jarvis_decision.outcome == DecisionOutcome.SUGGEST:
            response_parts.append(
                self._format_suggestion_response(gideon_analysis)
            )
        elif jarvis_decision.outcome == DecisionOutcome.CONFIRM:
            response_parts.append(
                self._format_confirmation_request(gideon_analysis)
            )
        
        # Unisci in risposta coerente
        return self._compose_natural_response(response_parts)
```

```python
class ChatInterface:
    """Interfaccia chat tipo WhatsApp con storico e contesto."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.conversation_history: List[Message] = []
        self.context = ConversationContext()
        self.operational_level = OperationalLevel.PASSIVE
    
    async def send_message(self, text: str) -> Message:
        """Invia messaggio utente."""
        user_msg = Message(
            role="user",
            content=text,
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
        self.conversation_history.append(user_msg)
        
        # Mantieni contesto multi-turno
        self.context.update(user_msg)
        
        return user_msg
    
    async def receive_response(
        self,
        response_data: ResponseData
    ) -> Message:
        """Ricevi risposta sistema."""
        assistant_msg = Message(
            role="assistant",
            content=response_data.text,
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            metadata={
                "operational_level": response_data.level,
                "confidence": response_data.confidence,
                "source": response_data.source  # GIDEON/JARVIS
            }
        )
        self.conversation_history.append(assistant_msg)
        
        # Aggiorna indicatore livello
        self._update_level_indicator(response_data.level)
        
        return assistant_msg
    
    def get_conversation_context(self, turns: int = 10) -> List[Message]:
        """Ottieni contesto ultimi N turni per multi-turno."""
        return self.conversation_history[-turns * 2:]
    
    def _update_level_indicator(self, level: OperationalLevel) -> None:
        """Aggiorna indicatore livello operativo nell'UI."""
        level_indicators = {
            OperationalLevel.PASSIVE: "ðŸ”µ PASSIVE",
            OperationalLevel.COPILOT: "ðŸŸ¡ COPILOT",
            OperationalLevel.PILOT: "ðŸŸ¢ PILOT"
        }
        self.operational_level = level
        self._render_indicator(level_indicators[level])
```

### 12.3 Multi-turno e Contesto

```python
class ConversationContext:
    """Mantiene contesto tra domande e risposte."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.topic: Optional[str] = None
        self.entities: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        self.pending_actions: List[Action] = []
        self.references: Dict[str, Any] = {}  # "quello", "esso", etc.
    
    def update(self, message: Message) -> None:
        """Aggiorna contesto con nuovo messaggio."""
        # Estrai entitÃ 
        new_entities = self._extract_entities(message.content)
        self.entities.update(new_entities)
        
        # Risolvi riferimenti
        resolved = self._resolve_references(message.content)
        
        # Aggiorna topic se cambiato
        self._update_topic(message.content)
    
    def resolve_reference(self, reference: str) -> Optional[Any]:
        """
        Risolve riferimenti a elementi precedenti.
        
        Esempio:
        User: "Analizza Chrome"
        User: "Chiudilo" â† "lo" = Chrome
        """
        reference_patterns = {
            "lo": self._get_last_singular_entity,
            "li": self._get_last_plural_entities,
            "quello": self._get_last_referenced,
            "questa": self._get_current_topic,
            "quella cosa": self._get_last_action_target
        }
        
        for pattern, resolver in reference_patterns.items():
            if pattern in reference.lower():
                return resolver()
        
        return None
    
    def get_full_context(self) -> Dict:
        """Restituisce contesto completo per processamento."""
        return {
            "topic": self.topic,
            "entities": self.entities,
            "pending_actions": [a.to_dict() for a in self.pending_actions],
            "conversation_summary": self._summarize_conversation()
        }
```

### 13.1 Kill-Switch Globale

```python
class KillSwitch:
    """
    Kill-switch globale per arresto immediato di tutte le operazioni.
    PrioritÃ  massima, non puÃ² essere ignorato.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._is_active = False
        self._activation_time: Optional[datetime] = None
        self._activation_reason: Optional[str] = None
        self._listeners: List[Callable] = []
    
    def activate(self, reason: str, source: str = "user") -> None:
        """
        Attiva kill-switch IMMEDIATAMENTE.
        Ferma tutte le operazioni in corso.
        """
        self._is_active = True
        self._activation_time = datetime.now()
        self._activation_reason = reason
        
        # Log critico
        logger.critical(f"ðŸ›‘ KILL SWITCH ACTIVATED by {source}: {reason}")
        
        # Notifica tutti i listener
        for listener in self._listeners:
            try:
                listener(reason)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Listener error during kill: {e}")
        
        # Forza stop di tutti i processi
        self._force_stop_all()
    
    def _force_stop_all(self) -> None:
        """Ferma forzatamente tutte le operazioni."""
        # Stop automation layer
        AutomationLayer.emergency_stop()
        
        # Stop execution queue
        ExecutionQueue.clear_and_stop()
        
        # Stop running routines
        RoutineManager.abort_all()
        
        # Disconnect external services
        ExternalConnector.disconnect_all()
    
    @property
    def is_active(self) -> bool:
        return self._is_active
    
    def deactivate(self, auth_code: str) -> bool:
        """Disattiva kill-switch (richiede autorizzazione)."""
        if not self._verify_auth(auth_code):
            logger.warning("Invalid auth code for kill-switch deactivation")
            return False
        
        self._is_active = False
        logger.info("Kill-switch deactivated")
        return True

# Triggers automatici
class AutomaticKillTriggers:
    """Condizioni che attivano automaticamente il kill-switch."""
    
    TRIGGERS = [
        # Errori critici consecutivi
        Trigger("consecutive_errors", threshold=5, window_seconds=60),
        
        # Resource exhaustion
        Trigger("memory_critical", threshold=0.95),
        Trigger("cpu_sustained_max", threshold=0.98, duration_seconds=30),
        
        # Security violations
        Trigger("unauthorized_access_attempts", threshold=3),
        Trigger("permission_escalation_attempt", threshold=1),
        
        # Anomaly detection
        Trigger("behavior_anomaly_score", threshold=0.9),
    ]
```

### 13.2 Rollback Automatico

```python
class AutomaticRollback:
    """
    Sistema di rollback automatico per errori o rischi.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.snapshot_manager = SnapshotManager()
        self.rollback_triggers = RollbackTriggers()
    
    async def evaluate_and_rollback(
        self,
        action_result: ActionResult
    ) -> Optional[RollbackResult]:
        """
        Valuta se necessario rollback e lo esegue.
        
        Trigger automatici:
        - Errore durante esecuzione
        - Risultato inaspettato
        - Risk score sopra threshold
        - User abort
        - System anomaly
        """
        needs_rollback = (
            not action_result.success or
            action_result.risk_score > 0.7 or
            self.rollback_triggers.is_triggered(action_result)
        )
        
        if needs_rollback:
            logger.warning(f"Auto-rollback triggered: {action_result.error}")
            
            # Recupera snapshot
            snapshot = self.snapshot_manager.get_latest(
                action_result.action_id
            )
            
            if snapshot:
                return await self._execute_rollback(snapshot)
            else:
                logger.error("No snapshot available for rollback")
                return RollbackResult(success=False, reason="No snapshot")
        
        return None
    
    async def _execute_rollback(self, snapshot: Snapshot) -> RollbackResult:
        """Esegue rollback allo snapshot."""
        steps_rolled_back = []
        
        for step in reversed(snapshot.steps):
            try:
                await step.rollback_action.execute()
                steps_rolled_back.append(step.id)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Rollback step failed: {step.id} - {e}")
                return RollbackResult(
                    success=False,
                    partial=True,
                    rolled_back=steps_rolled_back,
                    error=str(e)
                )
        
        return RollbackResult(
            success=True,
            rolled_back=steps_rolled_back
        )
```

### 13.3 Permessi Granulari

```python
class PermissionManager:
    """
    Sistema di permessi granulari per utenti e azioni.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.permissions_db = PermissionsDatabase()
        self.role_hierarchy = RoleHierarchy()
    
    # Definizione permessi
    PERMISSIONS = {
        # Sistema
        "system.read": "Lettura info sistema",
        "system.modify": "Modifica impostazioni",
        "system.admin": "Amministrazione completa",
        
        # Automation
        "automation.view": "Visualizza routine",
        "automation.run": "Esegui routine",
        "automation.create": "Crea routine",
        "automation.delete": "Elimina routine",
        
        # Applicazioni
        "apps.open": "Apri applicazioni",
        "apps.close": "Chiudi applicazioni",
        "apps.install": "Installa software",
        "apps.uninstall": "Disinstalla software",
        
        # File system
        "files.read": "Leggi file",
        "files.write": "Scrivi file",
        "files.delete": "Elimina file",
        "files.execute": "Esegui script",
        
        # Rete
        "network.access": "Accesso rete",
        "network.external": "Connessioni esterne",
        
        # Sicurezza
        "security.view_logs": "Visualizza log sicurezza",
        "security.manage": "Gestisci sicurezza",
        "security.killswitch": "Attiva/Disattiva kill-switch"
    }
    
    # Ruoli predefiniti
    ROLES = {
        "guest": ["system.read"],
        "user": ["system.read", "automation.view", "automation.run", 
                 "apps.open", "files.read"],
        "power_user": ["system.read", "system.modify", "automation.*",
                       "apps.*", "files.*", "network.access"],
        "admin": ["*"]  # Tutti i permessi
    }
    
    def check_permission(
        self,
        user: User,
        permission: str,
        resource: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> PermissionResult:
        """
        Verifica se utente ha permesso.
        
        Esempio:
        >>> pm.check_permission(user, "files.write", "/sensitive/data.txt")
        PermissionResult(granted=False, reason="Path restricted")
        """
        # Verifica permesso base
        user_permissions = self._get_user_permissions(user)
        
        if permission not in user_permissions and "*" not in user_permissions:
            return PermissionResult(
                granted=False,
                reason=f"Permission '{permission}' not granted"
            )
        
        # Verifica restrizioni su risorsa
        if resource:
            resource_check = self._check_resource_restrictions(
                user, permission, resource
            )
            if not resource_check.allowed:
                return PermissionResult(
                    granted=False,
                    reason=resource_check.reason
                )
        
        return PermissionResult(granted=True)
```

### 13.4 Validazione Logica Interna

```python
class InternalLogicValidator:
    """
    Validazione logica obbligatoria per azioni critiche.
    Verifica coerenza e sicurezza prima dell'esecuzione.
    """
    
    CRITICAL_ACTIONS = [
        "delete_file", "delete_folder",
        "uninstall_software",
        "modify_system_settings",
        "external_network_access",
        "execute_unknown_script",
        "mass_operation"  # >10 elementi
    ]
    
    async def validate(
        self,
        action: Action,
        context: ExecutionContext
    ) -> ValidationResult:
        """
        Esegue validazione multi-livello.
        
        Controlli:
        1. Coerenza con intent originale
        2. Permessi sufficienti
        3. Risk assessment
        4. Reversibility check
        5. Conflict detection
        """
        results = []
        
        # 1. Intent coherence
        coherence = await self._check_intent_coherence(action, context)
        results.append(("intent_coherence", coherence))
        
        # 2. Permission check
        permission = self._check_permissions(action, context.user)
        results.append(("permission", permission))
        
        # 3. Risk assessment
        risk = await self._assess_risk(action)
        results.append(("risk", risk))
        
        # 4. Reversibility
        reversible = self._check_reversibility(action)
        results.append(("reversibility", reversible))
        
        # 5. Conflicts
        conflicts = await self._detect_conflicts(action, context)
        results.append(("conflicts", conflicts))
        
        # Aggregazione risultati
        all_passed = all(r[1].passed for r in results)
        
        if not all_passed:
            failed = [r for r in results if not r[1].passed]
            return ValidationResult(
                valid=False,
                failed_checks=failed,
                recommendation=self._generate_recommendation(failed)
            )
        
        return ValidationResult(valid=True, checks=results)
    
    async def _assess_risk(self, action: Action) -> RiskAssessment:
        """Valuta rischio dell'azione."""
        risk_factors = {
            "irreversibility": 0.3 if not action.is_reversible else 0,
            "scope": self._calculate_scope_risk(action),
            "external_impact": 0.2 if action.has_external_impact else 0,
            "data_loss_potential": self._assess_data_loss_risk(action),
            "system_stability": self._assess_stability_impact(action)
        }
        
        total_risk = sum(risk_factors.values()) / len(risk_factors)
        
        return RiskAssessment(
            score=total_risk,
            factors=risk_factors,
            passed=total_risk < 0.7  # Threshold
        )
```

### 13.5 Audit Trail Completo

```python
class AuditTrail:
    """
    Audit trail completo con possibilitÃ  di replay decisionale.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, storage_path: Path):
        self.storage_path = storage_path
        self.current_session = self._generate_session_id()
    
    def log_event(
        self,
        event_type: AuditEventType,
        data: Dict[str, Any],
        severity: Severity = Severity.INFO
    ) -> AuditEntry:
        """
        Logga evento per audit.
        
        Tipi evento:
        - DECISION: Decisione JARVIS
        - ANALYSIS: Analisi GIDEON
        - EXECUTION: Esecuzione azione
        - PERMISSION: Check permessi
        - SECURITY: Eventi sicurezza
        - ERROR: Errori
        - USER_INPUT: Input utente
        """
        entry = AuditEntry(
            id=self._generate_entry_id(),
            timestamp=datetime.now(timezone.utc),
            session_id=self.current_session,
            event_type=event_type,
            severity=severity,
            data=data,
            context={
                "user": self._get_current_user(),
                "mode": self._get_operating_mode(),
                "system_state": self._capture_system_state()
            }
        )
        
        self._persist(entry)
        return entry
    
    async def replay_decision(
        self,
        decision_id: str
    ) -> DecisionReplay:
        """
        Replay di una decisione per analisi.
        Ricostruisce tutto il contesto e il processo decisionale.
        """
        # Recupera tutti gli eventi correlati
        events = self._get_related_events(decision_id)
        
        # Ricostruisci timeline
        timeline = self._build_timeline(events)
        
        # Simula decisione con contesto originale
        original_context = self._reconstruct_context(events)
        
        return DecisionReplay(
            decision_id=decision_id,
            timeline=timeline,
            original_context=original_context,
            events=events,
            can_simulate=True
        )
    
    def search(
        self,
        start_time: Optional[datetime] = None,
        end_time: Optional[datetime] = None,
        event_types: Optional[List[AuditEventType]] = None,
        severity_min: Optional[Severity] = None,
        user: Optional[str] = None
    ) -> List[AuditEntry]:
        """Cerca negli audit log con filtri."""
        query = AuditQuery(
            start_time=start_time,
            end_time=end_time,
            event_types=event_types,
            severity_min=severity_min,
            user=user
        )
        return self._execute_query(query)

# Formato entry audit
"""
{
  "id": "audit-20260128-143256-a1b2c3",
  "timestamp": "2026-01-28T14:32:56.789Z",
  "session_id": "session-20260128-140000",
  "event_type": "DECISION",
  "severity": "INFO",
  "data": {
    "decision_id": "dec-001",
    "intent": "optimize_performance",
    "outcome": "EXECUTE",
    "confidence": 0.87,
    "reasoning": "High success probability, low risk",
    "alternatives_considered": 3,
    "selected_action": "close_chrome_tabs"
  },
  "context": {
    "user": "admin",
    "mode": "PILOT",
    "system_state": {
      "ram_usage": 0.92,
      "cpu_usage": 0.45,
      "active_apps": ["Chrome", "VS Code", "Spotify"]
    }
  }
}
"""
```


### 14.1 Implementazione Ciclo

```python
class OperationalCycle:
    """
    Implementazione del ciclo operativo completo.
    """
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        orchestrator: Orchestrator,
        voice_system: VoiceInteractionSystem,
        automation: AutomationLayer,
        memory: MemorySystem,
        audit: AuditTrail
    ):
        self.orchestrator = orchestrator
        self.voice = voice_system
        self.automation = automation
        self.memory = memory
        self.audit = audit
        self.is_active = False
    
    async def run_cycle(self, user_input: str) -> CycleResult:
        """
        Esegue un ciclo operativo completo.
        """
        cycle_id = self._generate_cycle_id()
        start_time = datetime.now()
        
        try:
            # STEP 1: GiÃ  completato (attivazione vocale)
            self.audit.log_event(AuditEventType.USER_INPUT, {
                "cycle_id": cycle_id,
                "input": user_input
            })
            
            # STEP 2: Ascolto giÃ  completato, input ricevuto
            
            # STEP 3: Intent Detection (JARVIS)
            intent = await self._detect_intent(user_input, cycle_id)
            
            # STEP 4: Analisi Multi-Scenario (GIDEON)
            analysis = await self._analyze_scenarios(intent, cycle_id)
            
            # STEP 5: Decisione Finale (JARVIS)
            decision = await self._make_decision(intent, analysis, cycle_id)
            
            # STEP 6: Esecuzione (se approved)
            execution_result = None
            if decision.outcome == DecisionOutcome.EXECUTE:
                execution_result = await self._execute(decision, cycle_id)
            
            # STEP 7: Logging Completo
            self._log_cycle(cycle_id, intent, analysis, decision, execution_result)
            
            # STEP 8: Apprendimento
            await self._learn_from_cycle(
                cycle_id, intent, analysis, decision, execution_result
            )
            
            return CycleResult(
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                success=True,
                intent=intent,
                decision=decision,
                execution=execution_result,
                duration=(datetime.now() - start_time).total_seconds()
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.audit.log_event(AuditEventType.ERROR, {
                "cycle_id": cycle_id,
                "error": str(e),
                "traceback": traceback.format_exc()
            }, severity=Severity.ERROR)
            raise
    
    async def _detect_intent(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        cycle_id: str
    ) -> Intent:
        """Step 3: Intent Detection."""
        intent = await self.orchestrator.jarvis.interpreter.interpret(user_input)
        
        self.audit.log_event(AuditEventType.ANALYSIS, {
            "cycle_id": cycle_id,
            "step": "intent_detection",
            "intent": intent.to_dict()
        })
        
        return intent
    
    async def _analyze_scenarios(
        self,
        intent: Intent,
        cycle_id: str
    ) -> GideonAnalysis:
        """Step 4: Analisi Multi-Scenario."""
        context = self.memory.get_context()
        
        analysis = await self.orchestrator.gideon.analyze(
            intent=intent,
            context=context,
            generate_scenarios=True
        )
        
        self.audit.log_event(AuditEventType.ANALYSIS, {
            "cycle_id": cycle_id,
            "step": "scenario_analysis",
            "scenarios_generated": len(analysis.scenarios),
            "best_scenario": analysis.best_scenario.to_dict() if analysis.best_scenario else None
        })
        
        return analysis
    
    async def _make_decision(
        self,
        intent: Intent,
        analysis: GideonAnalysis,
        cycle_id: str
    ) -> JarvisDecision:
        """Step 5: Decisione Finale."""
        decision = await self.orchestrator.jarvis.decide(
            intent=intent,
            analysis=analysis,
            mode=self.orchestrator.mode_manager.current_mode
        )
        
        self.audit.log_event(AuditEventType.DECISION, {
            "cycle_id": cycle_id,
            "step": "final_decision",
            "decision": decision.to_dict()
        })
        
        return decision
    
    async def _execute(
        self,
        decision: JarvisDecision,
        cycle_id: str
    ) -> ExecutionResult:
        """Step 6: Esecuzione."""
        # Crea snapshot per rollback
        snapshot = await self.automation.create_snapshot()
        
        result = await self.automation.execute(
            action=decision.action,
            mode=decision.execution_mode
        )
        
        self.audit.log_event(AuditEventType.EXECUTION, {
            "cycle_id": cycle_id,
            "step": "execution",
            "action": decision.action.to_dict(),
            "result": result.to_dict(),
            "snapshot_id": snapshot.id
        })
        
        return result
    
    async def _learn_from_cycle(
        self,
        cycle_id: str,
        intent: Intent,
        analysis: GideonAnalysis,
        decision: JarvisDecision,
        execution: Optional[ExecutionResult]
    ) -> None:
        """Step 8: Apprendimento."""
        # Record in episodic memory
        self.memory.episodic.record_episode(
            event_type="operational_cycle",
            description=f"Cycle {cycle_id}: {intent.name}",
            context={
                "intent": intent.to_dict(),
                "scenarios": len(analysis.scenarios),
                "decision": decision.outcome.value,
                "executed": execution is not None,
                "success": execution.success if execution else None
            },
            outcome="success" if (execution and execution.success) else "failure"
        )
        
        # Update decision memory
        if execution:
            self.memory.decision.record_outcome(
                decision_id=decision.id,
                success=execution.success,
                actual_result=execution.result
            )
        
        # Trigger continuous learning
        await self.memory.learning.learn_from_interaction(
            Interaction(
                cycle_id=cycle_id,
                success=execution.success if execution else True,
                result=execution.result if execution else None,
                decision_id=decision.id
            )
        )
```

### 15.1 Simulazioni Parallele

```python
class ParallelSimulator:
    """Esegue simulazioni di scenari in parallelo."""
    
    def __init__(self, max_workers: int = 4):
        self.executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_workers)
        self.scenario_generator = ScenarioGenerator()
    
    async def simulate_parallel(
        self,
        context: Context,
        num_scenarios: int = 5
    ) -> List[SimulationResult]:
        """
        Genera e simula scenari in parallelo.
        
        Vantaggi:
        - Analisi piÃ¹ veloce
        - PiÃ¹ scenari esplorati
        - Confronto simultaneo
        """
        # Genera scenari
        scenarios = self.scenario_generator.generate(context, num_scenarios)
        
        # Simula in parallelo
        loop = asyncio.get_event_loop()
        tasks = [
            loop.run_in_executor(self.executor, self._simulate_one, s)
            for s in scenarios
        ]
        
        results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
        
        # Ordina per probabilitÃ  successo
        return sorted(results, key=lambda r: r.success_probability, reverse=True)
```

### 15.2 Ranking Scenari

```python
class ScenarioRanker:
    """Ranking scenari per rischio ed efficacia."""
    
    def rank(
        self,
        scenarios: List[Scenario],
        weights: Optional[Dict[str, float]] = None
    ) -> List[RankedScenario]:
        """
        Calcola ranking pesato degli scenari.
        
        Fattori:
        - success_probability: ProbabilitÃ  di successo
        - risk_score: Rischio (inverso)
        - efficiency: Efficienza (tempo/risorse)
        - reversibility: FacilitÃ  di rollback
        - user_impact: Impatto sull'utente
        """
        weights = weights or {
            "success_probability": 0.35,
            "risk_inverse": 0.25,
            "efficiency": 0.15,
            "reversibility": 0.15,
            "user_impact_inverse": 0.10
        }
        
        ranked = []
        for scenario in scenarios:
            score = (
                weights["success_probability"] * scenario.success_probability +
                weights["risk_inverse"] * (1 - scenario.risk_score) +
                weights["efficiency"] * scenario.efficiency_score +
                weights["reversibility"] * scenario.reversibility_score +
                weights["user_impact_inverse"] * (1 - scenario.user_impact)
            )
            ranked.append(RankedScenario(scenario=scenario, score=score))
        
        return sorted(ranked, key=lambda r: r.score, reverse=True)
```

### 15.3 Degradazione Automatica

```python
class AutomaticDegradation:
    """
    Degradazione automatica in caso di rischio alto.
    Riduce funzionalitÃ  per mantenere sicurezza.
    """
    
    DEGRADATION_LEVELS = [
        # Level 0: Full functionality
        DegradationLevel(
            name="FULL",
            risk_threshold=0.0,
            disabled_features=[]
        ),
        # Level 1: Reduced automation
        DegradationLevel(
            name="REDUCED_AUTOMATION",
            risk_threshold=0.5,
            disabled_features=["mass_operations", "silent_execution"]
        ),
        # Level 2: Confirm all
        DegradationLevel(
            name="CONFIRM_ALL",
            risk_threshold=0.7,
            disabled_features=["auto_execute", "background_routines"]
        ),
        # Level 3: Read only
        DegradationLevel(
            name="READ_ONLY",
            risk_threshold=0.85,
            disabled_features=["all_writes", "all_executions"]
        ),
        # Level 4: Safe mode
        DegradationLevel(
            name="SAFE_MODE",
            risk_threshold=0.95,
            disabled_features=["*"]  # Only queries allowed
        )
    ]
    
    def evaluate_and_degrade(
        self,
        current_risk: float
    ) -> DegradationResult:
        """Valuta rischio e applica degradazione appropriata."""
        for level in reversed(self.DEGRADATION_LEVELS):
            if current_risk >= level.risk_threshold:
                return self._apply_degradation(level)
        
        return DegradationResult(level="FULL", features_disabled=[])
```

### 15.4 Spiegazione Decisioni

```python
class DecisionExplainer:
    """Genera spiegazioni dettagliate delle decisioni."""
    
    async def explain(
        self,
        decision: JarvisDecision,
        analysis: GideonAnalysis,
        detail_level: str = "normal"
    ) -> str:
        """
        Genera spiegazione in linguaggio naturale.
        
        Livelli:
        - brief: Una frase
        - normal: Paragrafo con punti chiave
        - detailed: Spiegazione completa step-by-step
        """
        if detail_level == "brief":
            return self._brief_explanation(decision)
        elif detail_level == "detailed":
            return self._detailed_explanation(decision, analysis)
        else:
            return self._normal_explanation(decision, analysis)
    
    def _detailed_explanation(
        self,
        decision: JarvisDecision,
        analysis: GideonAnalysis
    ) -> str:
        """Spiegazione dettagliata step-by-step."""
        explanation = f"""
## Spiegazione Decisione

### 1. Richiesta Analizzata
Ho ricevuto la richiesta: "{decision.original_intent.text}"
Intent riconosciuto: {decision.original_intent.name} (confidence: {decision.original_intent.confidence:.2%})

### 2. Analisi GIDEON
Ho analizzato {len(analysis.scenarios)} scenari possibili:

{self._format_scenarios(analysis.scenarios)}

### 3. Valutazione Rischi
- Rischio complessivo: {analysis.risk_assessment.overall_risk:.2%}
- Fattori considerati: {', '.join(analysis.risk_assessment.factors.keys())}

### 4. Decisione JARVIS
Ho deciso di: **{decision.outcome.value}**

Reasoning: {decision.reasoning}

### 5. Percorso Alternativo
Se avessi scelto diversamente:
{self._format_alternatives(analysis.scenarios[1:3] if len(analysis.scenarios) > 1 else [])}
"""
        return explanation
```

### 15.5 Alert Predittivo

```python
class PredictiveAlertSystem:
    """Sistema di alert predittivo in tempo reale."""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.monitors = [
            ResourceMonitor(),
            BehaviorMonitor(),
            TrendAnalyzer(),
            AnomalyDetector()
        ]
        self.alert_queue: asyncio.Queue = asyncio.Queue()
    
    async def monitor_continuous(self) -> None:
        """Monitoraggio continuo con predizione."""
        while True:
            for monitor in self.monitors:
                result = await monitor.check()
                
                if result.predicted_issue:
                    alert = PredictiveAlert(
                        type=result.issue_type,
                        probability=result.probability,
                        time_to_issue=result.estimated_time,
                        severity=result.severity,
                        recommendation=result.recommendation
                    )
                    await self.alert_queue.put(alert)
            
            await asyncio.sleep(1)  # Check ogni secondo
    
    async def get_alert(self) -> PredictiveAlert:
        """Ottieni prossimo alert dalla coda."""
        return await self.alert_queue.get()

# Esempio alert
"""
ðŸš¨ ALERT PREDITTIVO

Tipo: RESOURCE_EXHAUSTION
ProbabilitÃ : 87%
Tempo stimato: 5 minuti

Problema previsto:
La RAM raggiungerÃ  il 95% nei prossimi 5 minuti
se Chrome continua al ritmo attuale.

Raccomandazione:
- Chiudere tab non utilizzati
- Oppure: aumentare swap file
"""
```

## 16. Output Tipo per Utente

> **Esempi di risposte che l'utente vedrÃ  dal sistema.**

```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚                        OUTPUT TIPO PER UTENTE                               â”‚
â”œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚                                                                             â”‚
â”‚  â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â” â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  ðŸ“Š ANALISI SCENARI                                                    â”‚ â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                                        â”‚ â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  "Ho analizzato 5 scenari possibili per la tua richiesta.             â”‚ â”‚
â”‚  â”‚   Il piÃ¹ sicuro ha probabilitÃ  di successo del 91%.                   â”‚ â”‚
â”‚  â”‚   Vuoi procedere con questo scenario?"                                â”‚ â”‚
â”‚  â”‚                                                                        â”‚ â”‚
â”‚  â”‚  [Dettagli]  [Procedi]  [Alternative]                                 â”‚ â”‚
```

### 17.1 Caratteristiche Chiave

| Caratteristica | Descrizione |
|----------------|-------------|
| **Autonomo** | Opera in modo indipendente, richiede intervento umano solo quando necessario |
| **Hands-free** | Controllo completo tramite voce, zero necessitÃ  di tastiera/mouse |
| **Cognitivo** | Ragionamento multi-step, analisi causale, predizione outcome |
| **Sicuro** | Multi-layer security, kill-switch, rollback, audit completo |
| **Predittivo** | Simulazione scenari futuri, risk assessment, alert preventivi |
| **Decisionale** | JARVIS decide in modo autonomo con validazione interna |
| **Esecutivo** | Automation Layer per esecuzione reale di azioni |
| **Apprendimento** | Memoria multi-livello, continuous learning, adattamento |

### 17.2 Confronto con Versione Cinematografica

```python
COMPARISON = {
    "Film GIDEON (The Flash)": {
        "capabilities": [
            "Conversazione naturale",
            "Analisi dati base",
            "Suggerimenti generici",
            "Interfaccia olografica"
        ],
        "limitations": [
            "Solo query/response",
            "Nessuna esecuzione autonoma",
            "Nessun sistema di sicurezza visibile",
            "Nessun apprendimento mostrato"
        ]
    },
```
